\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
CPP-\/\+API\+: The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} class forms an C++ interface to the functionality of the Open Asset Import Library.

Create an object of this class and call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} to import a file. If the import succeeds, the function returns a pointer to the imported data. The data remains property of the object, it is intended to be accessed read-\/only. The imported data will be destroyed along with the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} object. If the import fails, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} returns a nullptr pointer. In this case you can retrieve a human-\/readable error description be calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. You can call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} multiple times with a single \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. Actually, constructing \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} objects involves quite many allocations and may take some time, so it\textquotesingle{}s better to reuse them as often as possible.

If you need the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} to do custom file handling to access the files, implement \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_stream}{IOStream}} and supply an instance of your custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} implementation by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}{Set\+IOHandler()}} before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. If you do not assign a custom IO handler, a default handler using the standard C++ IO logic will be used.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
One \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance is not thread-\/safe. If you use multiple threads for loading, each thread should maintain its own \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. 
\end{DoxyNote}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2_importer_8hpp_source_l00120}{120}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2_importer_8hpp_source}{Importer.\+hpp}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Importer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} \&}]{other }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [delete]}}

Copy constructor.

This copies the configuration properties of another \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}}. If this \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} owns a scene it won\textquotesingle{}t be copied. Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} to start the import process. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3d65af5286ba22f46220a72a6eb2a1c9}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3d65af5286ba22f46220a72a6eb2a1c9}}

Constructor. Creates an empty importer object.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} to start the import process. The configuration property table is initially empty. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a31c6cd729b79d586504dabe30353e39a}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a31c6cd729b79d586504dabe30353e39a}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!ApplyPostProcessing@{ApplyPostProcessing}}
\index{ApplyPostProcessing@{ApplyPostProcessing}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ApplyPostProcessing()}{ApplyPostProcessing()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Apply\+Post\+Processing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apply post-\/processing to an already-\/imported scene.

This is strictly equivalent to calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} with the same flags. However, you can use this separate function to inspect the imported scene first to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Flags} & Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the post-\/processed data. This is still the same as the pointer returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. However, if post-\/processing fails, the scene could now be nullptr. That\textquotesingle{}s quite a rare case, post processing steps are not really designed to \textquotesingle{}fail\textquotesingle{}. To be exact, the \#ai\+Process\+\_\+\+Validate\+DS flag is currently the only post processing step which can actually cause the scene to be reset to nullptr.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The method does nothing if no scene is currently bound to the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2c207299ed05f1db1ad1e6dab005f719}{Importer}} instance. ~\newline
 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!ApplyPostProcessing@{ApplyPostProcessing}}
\index{ApplyPostProcessing@{ApplyPostProcessing}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ApplyPostProcessing()}{ApplyPostProcessing()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Apply\+Post\+Processing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apply post-\/processing to an already-\/imported scene.

This is strictly equivalent to calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} with the same flags. However, you can use this separate function to inspect the imported scene first to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Flags} & Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the post-\/processed data. This is still the same as the pointer returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. However, if post-\/processing fails, the scene could now be nullptr. That\textquotesingle{}s quite a rare case, post processing steps are not really designed to \textquotesingle{}fail\textquotesingle{}. To be exact, the \#ai\+Process\+\_\+\+Validate\+DS flag is currently the only post processing step which can actually cause the scene to be reset to nullptr.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The method does nothing if no scene is currently bound to the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2c207299ed05f1db1ad1e6dab005f719}{Importer}} instance. ~\newline
 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

A pointer to the post-\/processed data. This is still the same as the pointer returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. However, if post-\/processing fails, the scene could now be nullptr. That\textquotesingle{}s quite a rare case, post processing steps are not really designed to \textquotesingle{}fail\textquotesingle{}. To be exact, the \#ai\+Process\+\_\+\+Validate\+DS flag is currently the only post processing step which can actually cause the scene to be reset to nullptr.

\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!FreeScene@{FreeScene}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FreeScene()}{FreeScene()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Free\+Scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Frees the current scene.

The function does nothing if no scene has previously been read via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}{Free\+Scene()}} is called automatically by the destructor and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} itself. ~\newline
 \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!FreeScene@{FreeScene}}
\index{FreeScene@{FreeScene}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FreeScene()}{FreeScene()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Free\+Scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Frees the current scene.

The function does nothing if no scene has previously been read via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}{Free\+Scene()}} is called automatically by the destructor and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} itself. ~\newline
 \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Free\+Scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Frees the current scene.

The function does nothing if no scene has previously been read via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}{Free\+Scene()}} is called automatically by the destructor and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} itself. ~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Error\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns an error description of an error that occurred in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}.

Returns an empty string if no error occurred. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A description of the last error, an empty string if no error occurred. The string is never nullptr.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The returned function remains valid until one of the following methods is called\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a53dafc3046abc33365a07c605716c5d4}{Free\+Scene()}}.

\end{DoxyNote}

\index{GetExtensionList@{GetExtensionList}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetExtensionList()}{GetExtensionList()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Extension\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structai_string}{ai\+String}} \&}]{sz\+Out }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Get a full list of all file extensions supported by ASSIMP.

If a file extension is contained in the list this does of course not mean that ASSIMP is able to load all files with this extension --- it simply means there is an importer loaded which claims to handle files with this file extension. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sz\+Out} & String to receive the extension list. Format of the list\+: \char`\"{}$\ast$.\+3ds;$\ast$.\+obj;$\ast$.\+dae\char`\"{}. This is useful for use with the Win\+API call Get\+Open\+File\+Name(\+Ex). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Find the importer corresponding to a specific file extension.

This is quite similar to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a22bbe0ca29cc685b110b6853dd1e4157}{Is\+Extension\+Supported}} except a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_base_importer}{Base\+Importer}} instance is returned. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sz\+Extension} & Extension to check for. The following formats are recognized (BAH being the file extension)\+: \char`\"{}\+BAH\char`\"{} (comparison is case-\/insensitive), \char`\"{}.\+bah\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\ast$.\+bah\char`\"{} (wild card and dot characters at the beginning of the extension are skipped). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
nullptr if no importer is found 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Retrieves the IO handler that is currently set. You can use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ad2c940def9c4d01709e44a4e781e757d}{Is\+Default\+IOHandler()}} to check whether the returned interface is the default IO handler provided by ASSIMP. The default handler is active as long the application doesn\textquotesingle{}t supply its own custom IO handler via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}{Set\+IOHandler()}}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetMemoryRequirements()}{GetMemoryRequirements()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Memory\+Requirements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structai_memory_info}{ai\+Memory\+Info}} \&}]{in }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns the storage allocated by ASSIMP to hold the scene data in memory.

This refers to the currently loaded file, see \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em in} & Data structure to be filled. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The returned memory statistics refer to the actual size of the use data of the \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}}. Heap-\/related overhead is (naturally) not included. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!GetOrphanedScene@{GetOrphanedScene}}
\index{GetOrphanedScene@{GetOrphanedScene}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetOrphanedScene()}{GetOrphanedScene()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Orphaned\+Scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the scene loaded by the last successful call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} and releases the scene from the ownership of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. The application is now responsible for deleting the scene. Any further calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ae98429edc11286b8c91b33feac22fe9d}{Get\+Scene()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} will return nullptr -\/ until a new scene has been loaded via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Current scene or nullptr if there is currently no scene loaded 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Use this method with maximal caution, and only if you have to. By design, \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}}\textquotesingle{}s are exclusively maintained, allocated and deallocated by \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} and no one else. The reasoning behind this is the golden rule that deallocations should always be done by the module that did the original allocation because heaps are not necessarily shared. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} enforces you to delete the returned scene by yourself, but this will only be fine if and only if you\textquotesingle{}re using the same heap as assimp. On Windows, it\textquotesingle{}s typically fine provided everything is linked against the multithreaded-\/dll version of the runtime library. It will work as well for static linkage with \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}}. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!GetOrphanedScene@{GetOrphanedScene}}
\index{GetOrphanedScene@{GetOrphanedScene}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetOrphanedScene()}{GetOrphanedScene()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Orphaned\+Scene (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the scene loaded by the last successful call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} and releases the scene from the ownership of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. The application is now responsible for deleting the scene. Any further calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ae98429edc11286b8c91b33feac22fe9d}{Get\+Scene()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} will return nullptr -\/ until a new scene has been loaded via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Use this method with maximal caution, and only if you have to. The reasoning behind this is the golden rule that deallocations should always be done by the module that did the original allocation because heaps are not necessarily shared. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} enforces you to delete the returned scene by yourself, but this will only be fine if and only if you\textquotesingle{}re using the same heap as assimp. On Windows, it\textquotesingle{}s typically fine provided everything is linked against the multithreaded-\/dll version of the runtime library. It will work as well for static linkage with \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}}. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!GetOrphanedScene@{GetOrphanedScene}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetOrphanedScene()}{GetOrphanedScene()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Property\+Bool (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{sz\+Name,  }\item[{bool}]{b\+Error\+Return = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Get a boolean configuration property. Boolean properties are stored on the integer stack internally so it\textquotesingle{}s possible to set them via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a4af22a88eddf464d949a761149c72825}{Set\+Property\+Bool}} and query them with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a39e654c887f684cc12f792ca1daebfee}{Get\+Property\+Bool}} and vice versa. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac6f348464e03176bc6dd790226122b36}{Get\+Property\+Integer()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac6f348464e03176bc6dd790226122b36}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac6f348464e03176bc6dd790226122b36}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetPropertyInteger()}{GetPropertyInteger()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Get\+Property\+Integer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{sz\+Name,  }\item[{int}]{i\+Error\+Return = {\ttfamily 0xffffffff} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Get a configuration property. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sz\+Name} & Name of the property. All supported properties are defined in the ai\+Config.\+g header (all constants share the prefix AI\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+XXX). \\
\hline
{\em i\+Error\+Return} & Value that is returned if the property is not found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Current value of the property 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Property of different types (float, int, string ..) are kept on different lists, so calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}{Set\+Property\+Integer()}} for a floating-\/point property has no effect -\/ the loader will call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3a5f327bc30dfe95db6d8ff9297d4aab}{Get\+Property\+Float()}} to read the property, but it won\textquotesingle{}t be there. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac6f348464e03176bc6dd790226122b36}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac6f348464e03176bc6dd790226122b36}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!ReadFile@{ReadFile}}
\index{ReadFile@{ReadFile}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ReadFile()}{ReadFile()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Read\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{p\+File,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file and returns its contents if successful.

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer object keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, nullptr is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. The previous scene will be deleted during this call. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+File} & Path and filename to the file to be imported. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}{Apply\+Post\+Processing()}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the imported data, nullptr if the import failed. The pointer to the scene remains in possession of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} to take ownership of it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} is able to determine the file format of a file automatically. 
\end{DoxyNote}
Here is the caller graph for this function\+:

Reads the given file and returns its contents if successful.

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer object keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, nullptr is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. The previous scene will be deleted during this call. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+File} & Path and filename to the file to be imported. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}{Apply\+Post\+Processing()}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} to take ownership of it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} is able to determine the file format of a file automatically. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a04098fcae6dc74af19af7bdaa54ea68c}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a04098fcae6dc74af19af7bdaa54ea68c}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!ReadFileFromMemory@{ReadFileFromMemory}}
\index{ReadFileFromMemory@{ReadFileFromMemory}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ReadFileFromMemory()}{ReadFileFromMemory()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Read\+File\+From\+Memory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} void $\ast$}]{p\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{p\+Length,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{p\+Hint = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\char`\"{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file from a memory buffer and returns its contents if successful.

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer object keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, nullptr is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. The previous scene will be deleted during this call. Calling this method doesn\textquotesingle{}t affect the active \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Buffer} & Pointer to the file data \\
\hline
{\em p\+Length} & Length of p\+Buffer, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}{Apply\+Post\+Processing()}}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Hint} & An additional hint to the library. If this is a non empty string, the library looks for a loader to support the file extension specified by p\+Hint and passes the file to the first matching loader. If this loader is unable to completely the request, the library continues and tries to determine the file format on its own, a task that may or may not be successful. Check the return value, and you\textquotesingle{}ll know ... \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the imported data, nullptr if the import failed. The pointer to the scene remains in possession of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} to take ownership of it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is a straightforward way to decode models from memory buffers, but it doesn\textquotesingle{}t handle model formats that spread their data across multiple files or even directories. Examples include OBJ or MD3, which outsource parts of their material info into external scripts. If you need full functionality, provide a custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} to make \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} find these files and use the regular \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} API. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a04098fcae6dc74af19af7bdaa54ea68c}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a04098fcae6dc74af19af7bdaa54ea68c}}

A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. The previous scene will be deleted during this call. Calling this method doesn\textquotesingle{}t affect the active \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

Examples include OBJ or MD3, which outsource parts of their material info into external scripts. If you need full functionality, provide a custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} to make \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} find these files and use the regular \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} API.

\index{ReadFileFromMemory@{ReadFileFromMemory}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ReadFileFromMemory()}{ReadFileFromMemory()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} $\ast$ Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Read\+File\+From\+Memory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} void $\ast$}]{p\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{p\+Length,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{p\+Hint = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\char`\"{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file from a memory buffer and returns its contents if successful.

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer object keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, nullptr is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_ac217a8a4abfe22862dcbd5763fd16f25}{Get\+Error\+String()}}. The previous scene will be deleted during this call. Calling this method doesn\textquotesingle{}t affect the active \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Buffer} & Pointer to the file data \\
\hline
{\em p\+Length} & Length of p\+Buffer, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \mbox{\hyperlink{include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps}} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a59d8795629f6f39ccf9bc1967598e956}{Apply\+Post\+Processing()}}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Hint} & An additional hint to the library. If this is a non empty string, the library looks for a loader to support the file extension specified by p\+Hint and passes the file to the first matching loader. If this loader is unable to completely the request, the library continues and tries to determine the file format on its own, a task that may or may not be successful. Check the return value, and you\textquotesingle{}ll know ... \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the imported data, nullptr if the import failed. The pointer to the scene remains in possession of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} instance. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a46f442262c8a778f4d65331691dfe5f5}{Get\+Orphaned\+Scene()}} to take ownership of it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is a straightforward way to decode models from memory buffers, but it doesn\textquotesingle{}t handle model formats that spread their data across multiple files or even directories. Examples include OBJ or MD3, which outsource parts of their material info into external scripts. If you need full functionality, provide a custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} to make \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} find these files and use the regular \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a075ccc3ef0cd2b005a8f624e75ca8909}{Read\+File()}} API. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3846294ffe76d91a1d3096d22d7c6b7d}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3846294ffe76d91a1d3096d22d7c6b7d}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Set\+Extra\+Verbose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{b\+Do }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enables \char`\"{}extra verbose\char`\"{} mode.

\textquotesingle{}Extra verbose\textquotesingle{} means the data structure is validated after {\itshape every} single post processing step to make sure everyone modifies the data structure in a well-\/defined manner. This is a debug feature and not intended for use in production environments. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a9bb793072c84c784279d0f6e870bb42d}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a9bb793072c84c784279d0f6e870bb42d}}

This is a debug feature and not intended for use in production environments. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!SetIOHandler@{SetIOHandler}}
\index{SetIOHandler@{SetIOHandler}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetIOHandler()}{SetIOHandler()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Set\+IOHandler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} $\ast$}]{p\+IOHandler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Supplies a custom IO handler to the importer to use to open and access files. If you need the importer to use custom IO logic to access the files, you need to provide a custom implementation of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} and IOFile to the importer. Then create an instance of your custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} implementation and supply it by this function.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} takes ownership of the object and will destroy it afterwards. The previously assigned handler will be deleted. Pass nullptr to take again ownership of your \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} and reset \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} to use its default implementation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+IOHandler} & The IO handler to be used in all file accesses of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a1161f46318af18bb86dfe0fc3edea4df}}

Then create an instance of your custom \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_i_o_system}{IOSystem}} implementation and supply it by this function.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer}{Importer}} takes ownership of the object and will destroy it afterwards. The previously assigned handler will be deleted. {\footnotesize\ttfamily void Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Set\+Progress\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_progress_handler}{Progress\+Handler}} $\ast$}]{p\+Handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Supplies a custom progress handler to the importer. This interface exposes an \#\+Update() callback, which is called more or less periodically (please don\textquotesingle{}t sue us if it isn\textquotesingle{}t as periodically as you\textquotesingle{}d like it to have ...). This can be used to implement progress bars and loading timeouts. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Handler} & Progress callback interface. Pass nullptr to disable progress reporting. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Progress handlers can be used to abort the loading at almost any time. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Set\+Property\+Bool (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{sz\+Name,  }\item[{bool}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Set a boolean configuration property. Boolean properties are stored on the integer stack internally so it\textquotesingle{}s possible to set them via \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a4af22a88eddf464d949a761149c72825}{Set\+Property\+Bool}} and query them with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a39e654c887f684cc12f792ca1daebfee}{Get\+Property\+Bool}} and vice versa. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}{Set\+Property\+Integer()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}} 
\index{Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}!SetPropertyInteger@{SetPropertyInteger}}
\index{SetPropertyInteger@{SetPropertyInteger}!Assimp::Importer@{Assimp::Importer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetPropertyInteger()}{SetPropertyInteger()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Set\+Property\+Integer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{x64-_debug_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{sz\+Name,  }\item[{int}]{i\+Value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set an integer configuration property. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sz\+Name} & Name of the property. All supported properties are defined in the ai\+Config.\+g header (all constants share the prefix AI\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+XXX and are simple strings). \\
\hline
{\em i\+Value} & New value of the property \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the property was set before. The new value replaces the previous value in this case. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Property of different types (float, int, string ..) are kept on different stacks, so calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}{Set\+Property\+Integer()}} for a floating-\/point property has no effect -\/ the loader will call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a3a5f327bc30dfe95db6d8ff9297d4aab}{Get\+Property\+Float()}} to read the property, but it won\textquotesingle{}t be there. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}\label{class_assimp_1_1_importer_a2542eed3d5f491025c4095b4e55fa068}}

Unregisters a loader.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ValidateFlags()}{ValidateFlags()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Assimp\+::\+Importer\+::\+Validate\+Flags (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{p\+Flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Check whether a given set of post-\/processing flags is supported. 

Some flags are mutually exclusive, others are probably not available because your excluded them from your \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp}} builds. Calling this function is recommended if you\textquotesingle{}re unsure.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Flags} & Bitwise combination of the ai\+Post\+Process flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if this flag combination is fine. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
